ExTRaoRDinaRy

PaRT  i V  (B) – LocaL  GoVERnmEnT
Local Government Notifications
wxl 2311$19 – 2022 foieïn¾ ui 21 jeks nodod – 2022'12'21
no. 2311/19 – wEDnESDay, DEcEmBER 21, 2022
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
1A – PG6113 – 07 (2022/12)
PRaDEShiya  SaBha  waRiyaPoLa
IT is hereby notified for the public information that it has been decided under the resolution number 5(iii) held on 13.12.2022 
that the roads and lanes included in the following schedule should be declared as roads and lanes owned by the Wariyapola 
Pradeshiya Sabha, in terms of the functions assigned to the Pradeshiya Sabha in the North Western Province by the series of  
“Orders regarding the preparation of plans for the roads and lanes maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabhas in the North Western 
Province and the publication of advertisements showing the names of roads and lanes” published by the Hon. Governor, 
North Western Province in the Gazette Extraordinary No. 2238/35 dated 30
th July, 2021 to be read with Section 24 of the 
Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987.
 It is further notified that, if it is the opinion of the claimant party that any road or lane included in the Schedule will 
be pass through any land or part of a land, action should be taken to file a case in a proper court within three months from 
the date of this notification is published in order to confirm his ownership of that land.
 It is further notified that all the roads and lanes included in the schedule for which cases have not been filed in the 
Court before the expiry of the said three months period will be considered as roads and lanes owned by the Wariyapola 
Pradeshiya Sabha. 
                  T. M. Anura SudarShana,
Chairman,
Pradeshiya Sabha,
Wariyapola.
At Pradeshiya Sabha,
Wariyapola.
14
th December, 2022.
Resolution
    Wariyapola Pradeshiya Sabha proposes that the roads and lanes mentioned in the list included in the following schedule 
should be considered as roads and lanes maintained by the Wariyapola Pradeshiya Sabha under the provisions of the series of  
“Order regarding the preparation of plans for the roads and lanes maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabhas in the North Western 
Province and the publication of advertisements showing the names of roads and lanes” published by the Hon. Governor, 
North Western Province in the Extraordinary Gazette Notification No. 2238/35 dated 30
th July, 2021, and the provisions of 
Section 24(1) of the Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987.
